import Tabs from '@theme/Tabs';
import TabItem from '@theme/TabItem';

# Other Infographic Entities


## Angled Entry

<Tabs>
  <TabItem value="Preview">

![](./angled-entry.png#drawio)

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="Usage">
    
```js
import { AngledEntry } from '@dinghy/diagrams/entitiesInfoGraphic'

<AngledEntry/>

// or

import { extendStyle } from "@dinghy/base-components";
import { ANGLED_ENTRY } from '@dinghy/diagrams/entitiesInfoGraphic'

<Shape 
  {...props}
  _style={extendStyle(props, ANGLED_ENTRY)}
  />

```

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="Definition">
    
```js
{
  _style: {
    entity: 'shape=mxgraph.infographic.parallelogram;dx=5;html=1;fillColor=#10739E;strokeColor=none;shadow=0;fontSize=17;fontColor=#FFFFFF;align=center;fontStyle=1;whiteSpace=wrap;',
  },
  _width: 0,
  _height: 30,
}
```

  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

## Arc

<Tabs>
  <TabItem value="Preview">

![](./arc.png#drawio)

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="Usage">
    
```js
import { Arc } from '@dinghy/diagrams/entitiesInfoGraphic'

<Arc/>

// or

import { extendStyle } from "@dinghy/base-components";
import { ARC } from '@dinghy/diagrams/entitiesInfoGraphic'

<Shape 
  {...props}
  _style={extendStyle(props, ARC)}
  />

```

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="Definition">
    
```js
{
  _style: {
    entity: 'verticalLabelPosition=bottom;verticalAlign=top;html=1;shape=mxgraph.basic.arc;strokeColor=#10739E;strokeWidth=6;startAngle=0.3;endAngle=0.1;',
  },
  _original_width: 100,
  _original_height: 100,

}
```

  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

```js
  {...props}
  _style={extendStyle(props, ARC_LIST)}
  />

```

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem value="Definition">
    
```js
{
  _style: {
    entity: 'verticalLabelPosition=bottom;verticalAlign=top;html=1;shape=mxgraph.basic.partConcEllipse;fillColor=#10739E;strokeColor=#ffffff;startAngle=0.75;endAngle=0.08;arcWidth=0.16;strokeWidth=3;',
  },
  _width: 0,
  _height: 200,
}
```

  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

## Arrow Graph

<Tabs>
  <TabItem value="Preview">

![](./arrow-graph.png#drawio)

  </TabItem>

```js
import { extendStyle } from "@dinghy/base-components";
import { TRIANGLE_2 } from '@dinghy/diagrams/entitiesInfoGraphic'

<Shape 
  {...props}
  _style={extendStyle(props, TRIANGLE_2)}
  />

```

  </TabItem>

```js
    entity: 'triangle;direction=north;html=1;strokeWidth=4;fillColor=#F2931E;strokeColor=#ffffff;shadow=0;fontSize=10;fontColor=#FFFFFF;align=center;fontStyle=0;whiteSpace=wrap;spacing=10;',
  },
  _width: 0,
```
